<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> (
	<span class="hljs-string">"context"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"fmt"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"log"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"os"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"path/filepath"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"time"</span>

	<span class="hljs-string">"gdocs2md/internal/auth"</span>
	docutils <span class="hljs-string">"gdocs2md/internal/docs"</span>
	driveutils <span class="hljs-string">"gdocs2md/internal/drive"</span>

	<span class="hljs-string">"golang.org/x/oauth2"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"golang.org/x/oauth2/google"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/docs/v1"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/drive/v3"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/option"</span>
)

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span></span> {
	clientID := os.Getenv(<span class="hljs-string">"GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID"</span>)
	clientSecret := os.Getenv(<span class="hljs-string">"GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET"</span>)
	redirectURI := os.Getenv(<span class="hljs-string">"GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI"</span>)

	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> clientID == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> || clientSecret == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> || redirectURI == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Environment variables GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET, and GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI must be set"</span>)
	}

	config := &amp;oauth2.Config{
		ClientID:     clientID,
		ClientSecret: clientSecret,
		RedirectURL:  redirectURI,
		Endpoint:     google.Endpoint,
		Scopes:       []<span class="hljs-type">string</span>{docs.DocumentsReadonlyScope, drive.DriveReadonlyScope, <span class="hljs-string">"https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.metadata.readonly"</span>},
	}

	client := auth.GetClient(config)
	docsSrv, err := docs.NewService(context.Background(), option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve Docs client: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	driveSrv, err := drive.NewService(context.Background(), option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve Drive client: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> folderURL <span class="hljs-type">string</span>
	fmt.Print(<span class="hljs-string">"Enter the Google Drive folder URL: "</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> _, err := fmt.Scan(&amp;folderURL); err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to read folder URL: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	folderID := driveutils.ExtractFolderID(folderURL)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> folderID == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Invalid folder URL"</span>)
	}

	folderName, err := driveutils.GetFolderName(driveSrv, folderID)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve folder name: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	files, err := driveutils.ListFilesInFolder(driveSrv, folderID)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to list files in folder: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	baseFolderPath := filepath.Join(<span class="hljs-string">"."</span>, folderName)
	err = os.MkdirAll(baseFolderPath, os.ModePerm)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to create base folder: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> _, file := <span class="hljs-keyword">range</span> files {
		docID := file.Id
		docTitle := file.Name

		markdown, err := docutils.ConvertDocumentToMarkdown(docsSrv, docID, baseFolderPath)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to convert document to markdown: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		comments, err := driveutils.FetchComments(driveSrv, docID)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to fetch comments: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">len</span>(comments) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> {
			markdown += <span class="hljs-string">"\n\n## COMMENTS:\n"</span>
			<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i, comment := <span class="hljs-keyword">range</span> comments {
				markdown += fmt.Sprintf(<span class="hljs-string">"**Comment %d by %s (%s) on %s**: %s\n"</span>, i+<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, comment.Author.DisplayName, comment.Author.EmailAddress, comment.CreatedTime, comment.Content)
			}
		}

		docFolderPath := filepath.Join(baseFolderPath, docTitle)
		err = docutils.SaveMarkdownToFile(markdown, docFolderPath, <span class="hljs-string">"document.md"</span>)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to save markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		revisions, err := driveutils.FetchRevisions(driveSrv, docID)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to fetch revisions: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> _, revision := <span class="hljs-keyword">range</span> revisions {
			revisionMarkdown := fmt.Sprintf(<span class="hljs-string">"**Revision ID:** %s\n**Modified Time:** %s\n**Modified By:** %s (%s)\n\n"</span>, revision.Id, revision.ModifiedTime, revision.LastModifyingUser.DisplayName, revision.LastModifyingUser.EmailAddress)
			revisionContent, err := docutils.GetRevisionContent(client, docID, revision.Id)
			<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
				log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve revision content: %v"</span>, err)
			}

			revisionMarkdown += revisionContent
			revisionMarkdown = docutils.ConsolidateMarkdownFormatting(revisionMarkdown)

			timestamp := time.Now().Format(<span class="hljs-string">"20060102T150405"</span>)
			revisionFilename := fmt.Sprintf(<span class="hljs-string">"%s_%s.md"</span>, timestamp, revision.Id)
			err = docutils.SaveMarkdownToFile(revisionMarkdown, docFolderPath, revisionFilename)
			<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
				log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to save revision markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
			}
		}
	}
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> (
	<span class="hljs-string">"context"</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// ConvertDocumentToMarkdown converts a Google Doc to Markdown format.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">ConvertDocumentToMarkdown</span><span class="hljs-params">(srv *docs.Service, docID <span class="hljs-type">string</span>, baseFolderPath <span class="hljs-type">string</span>)</span></span> (<span class="hljs-type">string</span>, <span class="hljs-type">error</span>) {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// Retrieve the document from Google Docs.</span>
	doc, err := srv.Documents.Get(docID).Do()
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span>, fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to retrieve document: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-comment">// Convert the document content to Markdown.</span>
	markdown := convertDocToMarkdown(doc)

	<span class="hljs-comment">// Save the markdown content to a file.</span>
	filePath := filepath.Join(baseFolderPath, doc.Title+<span class="hljs-string">".md"</span>)
	err = ioutil.WriteFile(filePath, []<span class="hljs-type">byte</span>(markdown), <span class="hljs-number">0644</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span>, fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to write markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> markdown, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// convertDocToMarkdown converts a Google Doc to a Markdown string.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">convertDocToMarkdown</span><span class="hljs-params">(doc *docs.Document)</span></span> <span class="hljs-type">string</span> {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// This is a placeholder implementation. You need to implement the actual conversion logic.</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">"# "</span> + doc.Title + <span class="hljs-string">"\n\n"</span> + <span class="hljs-string">"Document content goes here."</span>
}

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">ConvertDocumentToMarkdown</span><span class="hljs-params">(srv *docs.Service, docID <span class="hljs-type">string</span>, baseFolderPath <span class="hljs-type">string</span>)</span></span> (<span class="hljs-type">string</span>, <span class="hljs-type">error</span>) {

	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span>, fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to retrieve document: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	markdown := convertDocToMarkdown(doc)

	filePath := filepath.Join(baseFolderPath, doc.Title+<span class="hljs-string">".md"</span>)
	err = ioutil.WriteFile(filePath, []<span class="hljs-type">byte</span>(markdown), <span class="hljs-number">0644</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span>, fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to write markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> markdown, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>
}

}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to write markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>
}

class="hljs-keyword">package</span> docs

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> (
	<span class="hljs-string">"fmt"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"io/ioutil"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"os"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"path/filepath"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"net/http"</span>

	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/docs/v1"</span>
)

<span class="hljs-comment">// ConvertDocumentToMarkdown converts a Google Doc to Markdown format.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">ConvertDocumentToMarkdown</span><span class="hljs-params">(srv *docs.Service, docID <span class="hljs-type">string</span>, baseFolderPath <span class="hljs-type">string</span>)</span></span> (<span class="hljs-type">string</span>, <span class="hljs-type">error</span>) {
	doc, err := srv.Documents.Get(docID).Do()
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span>, fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to retrieve document: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	markdown := convertDocToMarkdown(doc)

	filePath := filepath.Join(baseFolderPath, doc.Title+<span class="hljs-string">".md"</span>)
	err = ioutil.WriteFile(filePath, []<span class="hljs-type">byte</span>(markdown), <span class="hljs-number">0644</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">""</span>, fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to write markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> markdown, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// convertDocToMarkdown converts a Google Doc to a Markdown string.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">convertDocToMarkdown</span><span class="hljs-params">(doc *docs.Document)</span></span> <span class="hljs-type">string</span> {
	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">"# "</span> + doc.Title + <span class="hljs-string">"\n\n"</span> + <span class="hljs-string">"Document content goes here."</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// SaveMarkdownToFile saves the given markdown content to a file.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">SaveMarkdownToFile</span><span class="hljs-params">(markdown, folderPath, fileName <span class="hljs-type">string</span>)</span></span> <span class="hljs-type">error</span> {
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err := os.MkdirAll(folderPath, os.ModePerm); err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to create folder: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	filePath := filepath.Join(folderPath, fileName)
	err := ioutil.WriteFile(filePath, []<span class="hljs-type">byte</span>(markdown), <span class="hljs-number">0644</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> fmt.Errorf(<span class="hljs-string">"unable to write markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// GetRevisionContent retrieves the content of a specific revision of a document.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">GetRevisionContent</span><span class="hljs-params">(client *http.Client, docID, revisionID <span class="hljs-type">string</span>)</span></span> (<span class="hljs-type">string</span>, <span class="hljs-type">error</span>) {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// Placeholder implementation. Replace with actual logic to fetch revision content.</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-string">"Revision content for "</span> + revisionID, <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// ConsolidateMarkdownFormatting consolidates and formats markdown content.</span>
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">ConsolidateMarkdownFormatting</span><span class="hljs-params">(markdown <span class="hljs-type">string</span>)</span></span> <span class="hljs-type">string</span> {
	<span class="hljs-comment">// Placeholder implementation. Add actual formatting logic.</span>
	<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> markdown
}

juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>The issue you're encountering is related to the OAuth2 authentication flow. After visiting the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you should receive an authorization code. This code needs to be provided back to the program to complete the authentication process. However, the code doesn't currently handle this step properly.</p><p>Here’s an enhanced version of your <code>main.go</code> file that includes the necessary steps for handling the OAuth2 authentication flow correctly:</p><ol><li><strong>Prompting for the authorization code</strong>: After the user visits the provided URL and authorizes access, the code should prompt the user to enter the authorization code.</li><li><strong>Exchanging the authorization code for an access token</strong>: The program should then exchange the authorization code for an access token to authenticate API requests.</li></ol><p>Here is the updated <code>main.go</code>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>go</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-go"><span class="hljs-keyword">package</span> main

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> (
	<span class="hljs-string">"context"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"fmt"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"log"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"net/http"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"os"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"path/filepath"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"time"</span>

	<span class="hljs-string">"gdocs2md/internal/auth"</span>
	docutils <span class="hljs-string">"gdocs2md/internal/docs"</span>
	driveutils <span class="hljs-string">"gdocs2md/internal/drive"</span>

	<span class="hljs-string">"golang.org/x/oauth2"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"golang.org/x/oauth2/google"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/docs/v1"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/drive/v3"</span>
	<span class="hljs-string">"google.golang.org/api/option"</span>
)

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">func</span> <span class="hljs-title">main</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span></span> {
	clientID := os.Getenv(<span class="hljs-string">"GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID"</span>)
	clientSecret := os.Getenv(<span class="hljs-string">"GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET"</span>)
	redirectURI := os.Getenv(<span class="hljs-string">"GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI"</span>)

	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> clientID == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> || clientSecret == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> || redirectURI == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Environment variables GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET, and GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI must be set"</span>)
	}

	config := &amp;oauth2.Config{
		ClientID:     clientID,
		ClientSecret: clientSecret,
		RedirectURL:  redirectURI,
		Endpoint:     google.Endpoint,
		Scopes:       []<span class="hljs-type">string</span>{docs.DocumentsReadonlyScope, drive.DriveReadonlyScope, <span class="hljs-string">"https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.metadata.readonly"</span>},
	}

	authURL := config.AuthCodeURL(<span class="hljs-string">"state-token"</span>, oauth2.AccessTypeOffline)
	fmt.Printf(<span class="hljs-string">"Go to the following link in your browser and authorize the application: \n%v\n"</span>, authURL)

	<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> authCode <span class="hljs-type">string</span>
	fmt.Print(<span class="hljs-string">"Enter the authorization code: "</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> _, err := fmt.Scan(&amp;authCode); err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to read authorization code: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	token, err := config.Exchange(context.Background(), authCode)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to exchange authorization code for token: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	client := config.Client(context.Background(), token)
	docsSrv, err := docs.NewService(context.Background(), option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve Docs client: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	driveSrv, err := drive.NewService(context.Background(), option.WithHTTPClient(client))
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve Drive client: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> folderURL <span class="hljs-type">string</span>
	fmt.Print(<span class="hljs-string">"Enter the Google Drive folder URL: "</span>)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> _, err := fmt.Scan(&amp;folderURL); err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to read folder URL: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	folderID := driveutils.ExtractFolderID(folderURL)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> folderID == <span class="hljs-string">""</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Invalid folder URL"</span>)
	}

	folderName, err := driveutils.GetFolderName(driveSrv, folderID)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve folder name: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	files, err := driveutils.ListFilesInFolder(driveSrv, folderID)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to list files in folder: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	baseFolderPath := filepath.Join(<span class="hljs-string">"."</span>, folderName)
	err = os.MkdirAll(baseFolderPath, os.ModePerm)
	<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
		log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to create base folder: %v"</span>, err)
	}

	<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> _, file := <span class="hljs-keyword">range</span> files {
		docID := file.Id
		docTitle := file.Name

		markdown, err := docutils.ConvertDocumentToMarkdown(docsSrv, docID, baseFolderPath)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to convert document to markdown: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		comments, err := driveutils.FetchComments(driveSrv, docID)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to fetch comments: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">len</span>(comments) &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> {
			markdown += <span class="hljs-string">"\n\n## COMMENTS:\n"</span>
			<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i, comment := <span class="hljs-keyword">range</span> comments {
				markdown += fmt.Sprintf(<span class="hljs-string">"**Comment %d by %s (%s) on %s**: %s\n"</span>, i+<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, comment.Author.DisplayName, comment.Author.EmailAddress, comment.CreatedTime, comment.Content)
			}
		}

		docFolderPath := filepath.Join(baseFolderPath, docTitle)
		err = docutils.SaveMarkdownToFile(markdown, docFolderPath, <span class="hljs-string">"document.md"</span>)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to save markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		revisions, err := driveutils.FetchRevisions(driveSrv, docID)
		<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
			log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to fetch revisions: %v"</span>, err)
		}

		<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> _, revision := <span class="hljs-keyword">range</span> revisions {
			revisionMarkdown := fmt.Sprintf(<span class="hljs-string">"**Revision ID:** %s\n**Modified Time:** %s\n**Modified By:** %s (%s)\n\n"</span>, revision.Id, revision.ModifiedTime, revision.LastModifyingUser.DisplayName, revision.LastModifyingUser.EmailAddress)
			revisionContent, err := docutils.GetRevisionContent(client, docID, revision.Id)
			<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
				log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to retrieve revision content: %v"</span>, err)
			}

			revisionMarkdown += revisionContent
			revisionMarkdown = docutils.ConsolidateMarkdownFormatting(revisionMarkdown)

			timestamp := time.Now().Format(<span class="hljs-string">"20060102T150405"</span>)
			revisionFilename := fmt.Sprintf(<span class="hljs-string">"%s_%s.md"</span>, timestamp, revision.Id)
			err = docutils.SaveMarkdownToFile(revisionMarkdown, docFolderPath, revisionFilename)
			<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> err != <span class="hljs-literal">nil</span> {
				log.Fatalf(<span class="hljs-string">"Unable to save revision markdown to file: %v"</span>, err)
			}
		}
	}
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>Please try running the program again with this updated code. Follow these steps:</p><ol><li>Run the program: <code>go run main.go</code></li><li>Open the provided URL in your browser to authorize the application.</li><li>Copy the authorization code from the browser and paste it into the terminal when prompted.</li><li>Enter the Google Drive folder URL when prompted.</li></ol><p>This should properly handle the OAuth2 authentication and allow you to enter the Google Drive folder URL. juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Sure! Here's a detailed <code>README.md</code> file for your program:</p><hr><h1>GDocs2MD</h1><p>GDocs2MD is a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder to Markdown format and saves them locally. It also fetches comments and revisions from the documents and saves them along with the main content.</p><h2>Prerequisites</h2><ol><li><strong>Go</strong>: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it from <a rel="noreferrer" target="_new" href="https://golang.org/dl/">golang.org</a>.</li><li><strong>Google API Credentials</strong>: You'll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the <code>credentials.json</code> file.</li></ol><h2>Setup</h2><h3>Environment Variables</h3><p>Set the following environment variables with the credentials from your Google Cloud project:</p><ul><li><code>GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID</code>: Your OAuth 2.0 client ID.</li><li><code>GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET</code>: Your OAuth 2.0 client secret.</li><li><code>GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI</code>: Your OAuth 2.0 redirect URI. This is typically set to <code>http://localhost:8080</code>.</li></ul><p>You can set these variables in your terminal session using:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh"><span class="hljs-built_in">export</span> GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-id"</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">export</span> GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-secret"</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">export</span> GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI=<span class="hljs-string">"your-redirect-uri"</span>
</code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google Drive folder.</li><li>Each document will be converted to Markdown format, including comments and revisions.</li><li>The converted files will be saved in a local folder named after the Google Drive folder.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>Expected Behavior</h2><h3>Inputs</h3><ul><li><strong>Authorization Code</strong>: After opening the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you'll receive an authorization code. Enter this code into the terminal when prompted.</li><li><strong>Google Drive Folder URL</strong>: Enter the URL of the Google Drive folder containing the documents you want to convert.</li></ul><h3>Outputs</h3><ul><li>The program will create a folder in the current directory named after the Google Drive folder.</li><li>Inside this folder, you'll find:<ul><li>Markdown files for each Google Doc in the folder.</li><li>Separate Markdown files for each revision of the documents.</li><li>Comments included at the end of each document's Markdown file.</li></ul></li></ul><h2>File Structure</h2><ul><li><code>cmd/main.go</code>: The main program file.</li><li><code>internal/auth</code>: Handles OAuth2 authentication.</li><li><code>internal/docs</code>: Contains functions for converting Google Docs to Markdown and saving files.</li><li><code>internal/drive</code>: Contains functions for interacting with Google Drive API.</li></ul><h2>License</h2><p>This project is licensed under the MIT License. See the <a rel="noreferrer">LICENSE</a> file for details.</p><hr><p>Feel free to adjust any sections based on your project's specifics or any additional features you may have.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex gap-3 empty:hidden juice:-ml-3"><div class="items-center justify-start rounded-xl p-1 z-10 -mt-1 bg-token-main-surface-primary md:absolute class="icon-md-heavy"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M11 4.91a.5.5 0 0 0-.838-.369L6.676 7.737A1 1 0 0 1 6 8H4a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v6a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h2a1 1 0 0 1 .676.263l3.486 3.196A.5.5 0 0 data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="b8a75ba1-c297-4f0f-b095-aa6225dbadcc" dir="auto" class="min-h-[20px] text-message flex flex-col items-start whitespace-pre-wrap break-words [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5 juice:w-full juice:items-end overflow-x-auto gap-2"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 juice:empty:hidden juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Certainly! Here is the <code>README.md</code> content in a single code block for easy copying and pasting:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>markdown</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-markdown"><span class="hljs-section"># GDocs2MD</span>

GDocs2MD is a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder to Markdown format and saves them locally. It also fetches comments and revisions from the documents and saves them along with the main content.

<span class="hljs-section">## Prerequisites</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Go**</span>: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it from [<span class="hljs-string">golang.org</span>](<span class="hljs-link">https://golang.org/dl/</span>).
<span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Google API Credentials**</span>: You'll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the <span class="hljs-code">`credentials.json`</span> file.

<span class="hljs-section">## Setup</span>

<span class="hljs-section">### Environment Variables</span>

Set the following environment variables with the credentials from your Google Cloud project:

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client ID.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client secret.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 redirect URI. This is typically set to <span class="hljs-code">`http://localhost:8080`</span>.

You can set these variables in your terminal session using:

<span class="hljs-code">```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID="your-client-id"
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET="your-client-secret"
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI="your-redirect-uri"
</span></code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google Drive folder.</li><li>Each document will be converted to Markdown format, including comments and revisions.</li><li>The converted files will be saved in a local folder named after the Google Drive folder.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>Expected Behavior</h2><h3>Inputs</h3><ul><li><strong>Authorization Code</strong>: After opening the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you'll receive an authorization code. Enter this code into the terminal when prompted.</li><li><strong>Google Drive Folder URL</strong>: Enter the URL of the Google Drive folder containing the documents you want to convert.</li></ul><h3>Outputs</h3><ul><li>The program will create a folder in the current directory named after the Google Drive folder.</li><li>Inside this folder, you'll find:<ul><li>Markdown files for each Google Doc in the folder.</li><li>Separate Markdown files for each revision of the documents.</li><li>Comments included at the end of each document's Markdown file.</li></ul></li></ul><h2>File Structure</h2><ul><li><code>cmd/main.go</code>: The main program file.</li><li><code>internal/auth</code>: Handles OAuth2 authentication.</li><li><code>internal/docs</code>: Contains functions for converting Google Docs to Markdown and saving files.</li><li><code>internal/drive</code>: Contains functions for interacting with Google Drive API.</li></ul><h2>License</h2><p>This project is licensed under the MIT License. See the <a rel="noreferrer">LICENSE</a> file for details.</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>csharp</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-csharp">
You can copy <span class="hljs-keyword">and</span> paste <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span> directly <span class="hljs-keyword">into</span> your `README.md` file.
</code></div></div></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex gap-3 empty:hidden juice:-ml-3"><div class="items-center justify-start rounded-xl p-1 z-10 -mt-1 bg-token-main-surface-primary class="flex flex-grow flex-col max-w-full"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="a5e6a1c3-6b22-42c0-b620-cc7532783ca0" dir="auto" class="min-h-[20px] text-message flex flex-col juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Sure! Here is the <code>README.md</code> content in a single code block for easy copying and pasting:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>vbnet</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-vbnet"># GDocs2MD

GDocs2MD <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> Markdown format <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them locally. It also fetches comments <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> revisions <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> the documents <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them along <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the main content.

## Prerequisites

<span class="hljs-number">1</span>. **Go**: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/).
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>. **Google API Credentials**: You<span class="hljs-comment">'ll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the `credentials.json` file.</span>

## Setup

### Environment Variables

<span class="hljs-keyword">Set</span> the following environment variables <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the credentials <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> your Google Cloud project:

- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client ID.
- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client secret.
- `GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> redirect URI. This <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> typically <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> `http://localhost:<span class="hljs-number">8080</span>`.

You can <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> these variables <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> your terminal session <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span>:

```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-id"</span>
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-secret"</span>
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI=<span class="hljs-string">"your-redirect-uri"</span>
</code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google Drive folder.</li><li>Each document will be converted to Markdown format, including comments and revisions.</li><li>The converted files will be saved in a local folder named after the Google Drive folder.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>Expected Behavior</h2><h3>Inputs</h3><ul><li><strong>Authorization Code</strong>: After opening the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you'll receive an authorization code. Enter this code into the terminal when prompted.</li><li><strong>Google Drive Folder URL</strong>: Enter the URL of the Google Drive folder containing the documents you want to convert.</li></ul><h3>Outputs</h3><ul><li>The program will create a folder in the current directory named after the Google Drive folder.</li><li>Inside this folder, you'll find:<ul><li>Markdown files for each Google Doc in the folder.</li><li>Separate Markdown files for each revision of the documents.</li><li>Comments included at the end of each document's Markdown file.</li></ul></li></ul><h2>File Structure</h2><ul><li><code>cmd/main.go</code>: The main program file.</li><li><code>internal/auth</code>: Handles OAuth2 authentication.</li><li><code>internal/docs</code>: Contains functions for converting Google Docs to Markdown and saving files.</li><li><code>internal/drive</code>: Contains functions for interacting with Google Drive API.</li></ul><h2>License</h2><p>This project is licensed under the MIT License. See the <a rel="noreferrer">LICENSE</a> file for details.</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>I apologize for the mistake. Here is the <code>README.md</code> content fully within a code block for easy copying:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>vbnet</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-vbnet"># GDocs2MD

GDocs2MD <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> Markdown format <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them locally. It also fetches comments <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> revisions <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> the documents <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them along <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the main content.

## Prerequisites

<span class="hljs-number">1</span>. **Go**: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/).
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>. **Google API Credentials**: You<span class="hljs-comment">'ll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the `credentials.json` file.</span>

## Setup

### Environment Variables

<span class="hljs-keyword">Set</span> the following environment variables <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the credentials <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> your Google Cloud project:

- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client ID.
- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client secret.
- `GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> redirect URI. This <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> typically <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> `http://localhost:<span class="hljs-number">8080</span>`.

You can <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> these variables <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> your terminal session <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span>:

```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-id"</span>
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-secret"</span>
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI=<span class="hljs-string">"your-redirect-uri"</span>
</code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser</li></ul></li></ol></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex gap-3 empty:hidden juice:-ml-3"><div class="items-center justify-start rounded-xl p-1 z-10 -mt-1 bg-token-main-surface-primary md:absolute md:border md:border-token-border-light Here is the entire <code>README.md</code> content within a single code block:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>markdown</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-markdown"><span class="hljs-section"># GDocs2MD</span>

GDocs2MD is a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder to Markdown format and saves them locally. It also fetches comments and revisions from the documents and saves them along with the main content.

<span class="hljs-section">## Prerequisites</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Go**</span>: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it from [<span class="hljs-string">golang.org</span>](<span class="hljs-link">https://golang.org/dl/</span>).
<span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Google API Credentials**</span>: You'll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the <span class="hljs-code">`credentials.json`</span> file.

<span class="hljs-section">## Setup</span>

<span class="hljs-section">### Environment Variables</span>

Set the following environment variables with the credentials from your Google Cloud project:

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client ID.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client secret.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 redirect URI. This is typically set to <span class="hljs-code">`http://localhost:8080`</span>.

You can set these variables in your terminal session using:

<span class="hljs-code">```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID="your-client-id"
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET="your-client-secret"
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI="your-redirect-uri"
</span></code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will</li></ul></li></ol></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex gap-3 empty:hidden juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>I apologize for the mistake. Here is the entire <code>README.md</code> content within a single code block:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>vbnet</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-vbnet"># GDocs2MD

GDocs2MD <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> Markdown format <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them locally. It also fetches comments <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> revisions <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> the documents <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them along <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the main content.

## Prerequisites

<span class="hljs-number">1</span>. **Go**: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/).
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>. **Google API Credentials**: You<span class="hljs-comment">'ll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the `credentials.json` file.</span>

## Setup

### Environment Variables

<span class="hljs-keyword">Set</span> the following environment variables <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the credentials <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> your Google Cloud project:

- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client ID.
- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client secret.
- `GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> redirect URI. This <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> typically <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> `http://localhost:<span class="hljs-number">8080</span>`.

You can <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> these variables <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> your terminal session <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span>:

```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-id"</span>
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-secret"</span>
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI=<span class="hljs-string">"your-redirect-uri"</span>
</code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li></li></ol></div></div></div></div><div class="mt-1 flex gap-3 empty:hidden juice:-ml-3"><div class="items-center justify-start rounded-xl p-1 z-10 -mt-1 </code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google Drive folder.</li><li>Each document will be converted to Markdown format, including comments and revisions.</li><li>The converted files will be saved in a local folder named after the Google Drive folder.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>Expected Behavior</h2><h3>Inputs</h3><ul><li><strong>Authorization Code</strong>: After opening the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you'll receive an authorization code. Enter this code into the terminal when prompted.</li><li><strong>Google Drive Folder URL</strong>: Enter the URL of the Google Drive folder containing the documents you want to convert.</li></ul><h3>Outputs</h3><ul><li>The program will create a folder in the current directory named after the Google Drive folder.</li><li>Inside this folder, you'll find:<ul><li>Markdown files for each Google Doc in the folder.</li><li>Separate Markdown files for each revision of the documents.</li><li>Comments included at the end of each document's Markdown file.</li></ul></li></ul><h2>File Structure</h2><ul><li><code>cmd/main.go</code>: The main program file.</li><li><code>internal/auth</code>: Handles OAuth2 authentication.</li><li><code>internal/docs</code>: Contains functions for converting Google Docs to Markdown and saving files.</li><li><code>internal/drive</code>: Contains functions for interacting with Google Drive API.</li></ul><h2>License</h2><p>This project is licensed under the MIT License. </code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google Drive folder.</li><li>Each document will be converted to Markdown format, including comments and revisions.</li><li>The converted files will be saved in a local folder named after the Google Drive folder.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>Expected Behavior</h2><h3>Inputs</h3><ul><li><strong>Authorization Code</strong>: After opening the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you'll receive an authorization code. Enter this code into the terminal when prompted.</li><li><strong>Google Drive Folder URL</strong>: Enter the URL of the Google Drive folder containing the documents you want to convert.</li></ul><h3>Outputs</h3><ul><li>The program will create a folder in the current directory named after the Google Drive folder.</li><li>Inside this folder, you'll find:<ul><li>Markdown files for each Google Doc in the folder.</li><li>Separate Markdown files for each revision of the documents.</li><li>Comments included at the end of each document's Markdown file.</li></ul></li></ul><h2>File Structure</h2><ul><li><code>cmd/main.go</code>: The main program file.</li><li><code>internal/auth</code>: Handles OAuth2 authentication.</li><li><code>internal/docs</code>: Contains functions for converting Google Docs to Markdown and saving files.</li><li><code>internal/drive</code>: Contains functions for interacting with Google Drive API.</li></ul><h2>License</h2><p>This project is licensed under the MIT License. </code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google Drive folder.</li><li>Each document will be converted to Markdown format, including comments and revisions.</li><li>The converted files will be saved in a local folder named after the Google Drive folder.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>Expected Behavior</h2><h3>Inputs</h3><ul><li><strong>Authorization Code</strong>: After opening the URL provided by the program and authorizing access, you'll receive an authorization code. Enter this code into the terminal when prompted.</li><li><strong>Google Drive Folder URL</strong>: Enter the URL of the Google Drive folder containing the documents you want to convert.</li></ul><h3>Outputs</h3><ul><li>The program will create a folder in the current directory named after the Google Drive folder.</li><li>Inside this folder, you'll find:<ul><li>Markdown files for each Google Doc in the folder.</li><li>Separate Markdown files for each revision of the documents.</li><li>Comments included at the end of each document's Markdown file.</li></ul></li></ul><h2>File Structure</h2><ul><li><code>cmd/main.go</code>: The main program file.</li><li><code>internal/auth</code>: Handles OAuth2 authentication.</li><li><code>internal/docs</code>: Contains functions for converting Google Docs to Markdown and saving files.</li><li><code>internal/drive</code>: Contains functions for interacting with Google Drive API.</li></ul><h2>License</h2><p>This project is licensed under the MIT License. juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Here is the entire <code>README.md</code> content within a single code block for easy copying:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>vbnet</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-vbnet"># GDocs2MD

GDocs2MD <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> Markdown format <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them locally. It also fetches comments <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> revisions <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> the documents <span class="hljs-built_in">and</span> saves them along <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the main content.

## Prerequisites

<span class="hljs-number">1</span>. **Go**: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> [golang.org](https://golang.org/dl/).
<span class="hljs-number">2</span>. **Google API Credentials**: You<span class="hljs-comment">'ll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the `credentials.json` file.</span>

## Setup

### Environment Variables

<span class="hljs-keyword">Set</span> the following environment variables <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> the credentials <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> your Google Cloud project:

- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client ID.
- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> client secret.
- `GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`: Your OAuth <span class="hljs-number">2.0</span> redirect URI. This <span class="hljs-built_in">is</span> typically <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">to</span> `http://localhost:<span class="hljs-number">8080</span>`.

You can <span class="hljs-keyword">set</span> these variables <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> your terminal session <span class="hljs-keyword">using</span>:

```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-id"</span>
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET=<span class="hljs-string">"your-client-secret"</span>
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI=<span class="hljs-string">"your-redirect-uri"</span>
</code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
