Let's try another approach. I'll provide the <code>README.md</code> content in a downloadable format.</p><p>Here's the content you need:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>markdown</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-markdown"><span class="hljs-section"># GDocs2MD</span>

GDocs2MD is a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder to Markdown format and saves them locally. It also fetches comments and revisions from the documents and saves them along with the main content.

<span class="hljs-section">## Prerequisites</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Go**</span>: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it from [<span class="hljs-string">golang.org</span>](<span class="hljs-link">https://golang.org/dl/</span>).
<span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Google API Credentials**</span>: You'll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the <span class="hljs-code">`credentials.json`</span> file.

<span class="hljs-section">## Setup</span>

<span class="hljs-section">### Environment Variables</span>

Set the following environment variables with the credentials from your Google Cloud project:

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client ID.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client secret.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 redirect URI. This is typically set to <span class="hljs-code">`http://localhost:8080`</span>.

You can set these variables in your terminal session using:

<span class="hljs-code">```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID="your-client-id"
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET="your-client-secret"
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI="your-redirect-uri"
</span></code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder juice:first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>I can provide the <code>README.md</code> content in a downloadable text file. Here is the complete content as a downloadable file.</p><p>I'll generate a <code>README.md</code> file for you.</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>markdown</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-markdown"><span class="hljs-section"># GDocs2MD</span>

GDocs2MD is a command-line tool that converts Google Docs documents within a specified Google Drive folder to Markdown format and saves them locally. It also fetches comments and revisions from the documents and saves them along with the main content.

<span class="hljs-section">## Prerequisites</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Go**</span>: Ensure you have Go installed. You can download it from [<span class="hljs-string">golang.org</span>](<span class="hljs-link">https://golang.org/dl/</span>).
<span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Google API Credentials**</span>: You'll need a Google Cloud project with the Google Drive and Google Docs APIs enabled. Create OAuth 2.0 credentials and download the <span class="hljs-code">`credentials.json`</span> file.

<span class="hljs-section">## Setup</span>

<span class="hljs-section">### Environment Variables</span>

Set the following environment variables with the credentials from your Google Cloud project:

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client ID.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 client secret.
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-code">`GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI`</span>: Your OAuth 2.0 redirect URI. This is typically set to <span class="hljs-code">`http://localhost:8080`</span>.

You can set these variables in your terminal session using:

<span class="hljs-code">```sh
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID="your-client-id"
export GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET="your-client-secret"
export GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI="your-redirect-uri"
</span></code></div></div></pre><h3>Install Dependencies</h3><p>Run the following command to install the required dependencies:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go mod tidy
</code></div></div></pre><h2>Usage</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Run the Program</strong>:</p><pre><div class="dark bg-gray-950 rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium"><div class="flex items-center relative text-token-text-secondary bg-token-main-surface-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md"><span>sh</span><div class="flex items-center"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="icon-sm"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v9a3 3 0 0 1-3 3h-2v2a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H5a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-9a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h2zm2 2h5a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v5h2a1 1 0 0 0 1-1V5a1 1 0 0 0-1-1h-9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1zM5 9a1 1 0 0 0-1 1v9a1 1 0 0 0 1 1h9a1 1 0 0 0 1-1v-9a1 1 0 0 0-1-1z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-sh">go run cmd/main.go
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Authorize the Application</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will prompt you to open a URL in your browser.</li><li>Open the URL, log in to your Google account, and grant the necessary permissions.</li><li>Copy the authorization code provided and paste it back into the terminal.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Enter the Google Drive Folder URL</strong>:</p><ul><li>After authentication, the program will prompt you to enter the URL of the Google Drive folder you want to process.</li><li>Paste the folder URL into the terminal and press Enter.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Conversion Process</strong>:</p><ul><li>The program will retrieve the documents from the specified Google</li></ul></li></ol></div></div></div></div><div
